\"text\": \"The GroupCoordinator in Apache Kafka is implemented across multiple files in the group-coordinator module. The core interface is defined in GroupCoordinator.java, which specifies the key operations: joinGroup, syncGroup, and consumerGroupHeartbeat. The main implementation is in GroupCoordinatorService.java, which delegates to GroupCoordinatorShard.java for actual request handling.\\n\\nThe GroupMetadataManager (GroupMetadataManager.java) is the central state machine for managing group metadata. It handles both classic groups and modern consumer groups, managing their state transitions and lifecycle.\\n\\nClassic groups use a state machine with five states defined in ClassicGroupState.java: EMPTY (initial state), PREPARING_REBALANCE (when rebalance is triggered), COMPLETING_REBALANCE (after assignment from leader), STABLE (ready for consumption), and DEAD (when group is removed). ClassicGroup.java implements the group object with transitionTo() method for state transitions, while ClassicGroupMember.java represents individual members with sessionTimeoutMs tracking.\\n\\nModern consumer groups use ConsumerGroup.java with its own state machine (enum ConsumerGroupState with states like EMPTY, ASSIGNING, RECONCILING, STABLE) and ConsumerGroupMember.java for members. The ModernGroup.java base class manages assignment epochs via targetAssignmentEpoch, and MemberState.java defines member states.\\n\\nShare groups are handled by ShareGroup.java and ShareGroupMember.java, while Streams groups use StreamsGroup.java and StreamsGroupMember.java. All groups extend ModernGroup.java which provides common functionality for the modern group protocol.\\n\\nThe request handlers are located in GroupCoordinatorShard.java:\\n- handleJoinGroup: Processes JoinGroup requests, triggering the rebalance protocol\\n- handleSyncGroup: Processes SyncGroup requests to complete rebalance and assign partitions\\n- consumerGroupHeartbeat: Handles the modern heartbeat protocol for consumer groups\\n\\nHeartbeat expiry detection is implemented through timeout scheduling in GroupMetadataManager.java:\\n- rescheduleClassicGroupMemberHeartbeat: Reschedules heartbeat timeouts for classic group members based on sessionTimeoutMs\\n- scheduleConsumerGroupSessionTimeout: Schedules session timeout for modern consumer group members\\n- scheduleShareGroupSessionTimeout: Schedules session timeout for share group members\\n\\nThe assignment process is managed through TargetAssignmentBuilder classes which manage the assignment epoch increments. CurrentAssignmentBuilder classes in consumer and share packages track the current assignment state.\\n\\nGroupCoordinatorConfig.java defines all configuration parameters including heartbeat intervals and session timeouts. The metrics are tracked in GroupCoordinatorMetrics.java, GroupCoordinatorMetricsShard.java, and GroupCoordinatorRuntimeMetrics.java, recording counts of groups in each state.\\n\\nPartition assignors (RangeAssignor.java, UniformAssignor.java, SimpleAssignor.java) implement the assignment strategy when the group leader performs rebalancing.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":6027,"cache_read_input_tokens":79469,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":6027},"output_tokens":4,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"5a6c07e3-624f-40fb-8ed7-29a4e5c4f067","uuid":"c9b5b2e7-794b-4fa3-8958-d2aa1202430b"}

\"text\": \"The GroupCoordinator in Apache Kafka is implemented across multiple files in the group-coordinator module. The core interface is defined in GroupCoordinator.java, which specifies the key operations: joinGroup, syncGroup, and consumerGroupHeartbeat. The main implementation is in GroupCoordinatorService.java, which delegates to GroupCoordinatorShard.java for actual request handling.\\n\\nThe GroupMetadataManager (GroupMetadataManager.java) is the central state machine for managing group metadata. It handles both classic groups and modern consumer groups, managing their state transitions and lifecycle.\\n\\nClassic groups use a state machine with five states defined in ClassicGroupState.java: EMPTY (initial state), PREPARING_REBALANCE (when rebalance is triggered), COMPLETING_REBALANCE (after assignment from leader), STABLE (ready for consumption), and DEAD (when group is removed). ClassicGroup.java implements the group object with transitionTo() method for state transitions, while ClassicGroupMember.java represents individual members with sessionTimeoutMs tracking.\\n\\nModern consumer groups use ConsumerGroup.java with its own state machine (enum ConsumerGroupState with states like EMPTY, ASSIGNING, RECONCILING, STABLE) and ConsumerGroupMember.java for members. The ModernGroup.java base class manages assignment epochs via targetAssignmentEpoch, and MemberState.java defines member states.\\n\\nShare groups are handled by ShareGroup.java and ShareGroupMember.java, while Streams groups use StreamsGroup.java and StreamsGroupMember.java. All groups extend ModernGroup.java which provides common functionality for the modern group protocol.\\n\\nThe request handlers are located in GroupCoordinatorShard.java:\\n- handleJoinGroup: Processes JoinGroup requests, triggering the rebalance protocol\\n- handleSyncGroup: Processes SyncGroup requests to complete rebalance and assign partitions\\n- consumerGroupHeartbeat: Handles the modern heartbeat protocol for consumer groups\\n\\nHeartbeat expiry detection is implemented through timeout scheduling in GroupMetadataManager.java:\\n- rescheduleClassicGroupMemberHeartbeat: Reschedules heartbeat timeouts for classic group members based on sessionTimeoutMs\\n- scheduleConsumerGroupSessionTimeout: Schedules session timeout for modern consumer group members\\n- scheduleShareGroupSessionTimeout: Schedules session timeout for share group members\\n\\nThe assignment process is managed through TargetAssignmentBuilder classes which manage the assignment epoch increments. CurrentAssignmentBuilder classes in consumer and share packages track the current assignment state.\\n\\nGroupCoordinatorConfig.java defines all configuration parameters including heartbeat intervals and session timeouts. The metrics are tracked in GroupCoordinatorMetrics.java, GroupCoordinatorMetricsShard.java, and GroupCoordinatorRuntimeMetrics.java, recording counts of groups in each state.\\n\\nPartition assignors (RangeAssignor.java, UniformAssignor.java, SimpleAssignor.java) implement the assignment strategy when the group leader performs rebalancing.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
